    "hydrogen is the simplest atom , with the nucleus surrounded by a single electron .",
    "a hydrogenlike atom is a bound system isoelectronic with hydrogen , consisting of any atomic nucleus and an electron . except for the hydrogen itself ,",
    "hydrogenlike atoms carry a positive charge @xmath5 , where @xmath6 is the electron charge and @xmath7 is the nuclear charge number of the atom . examples of hydrogenlike atoms are he@xmath8 , li@xmath9 , u@xmath10 .",
    "the simplicity of hydrogenlike atoms makes them an ideal testing ground for extending the theory based on the principles of quantum electrodynamics ( qed ) up to the utmost precision @xcite .",
    "the creation of the modern qed goes back to the late 1940s , when lamb and retherford discovered the @xmath11-@xmath12 splitting in hydrogen , which is now known as the lamb shift .",
    "the first calculation of the lamb shift was performed by hans bethe @xcite who used kramer s idea of the mass renormalization .",
    "the rigorous formalism of qed was developed by dyson , feynman , schwinger and tomonaga , who proved that all infinities in the theory can be removed by the so - called renormalization procedure .",
    "all calculations in qed are based on the perturbation expansion in powers of the fine structure constant @xmath13 .",
    "the individual terms of the perturbation series can be conveniently represented in terms of the so - called feynman diagrams , with the power of @xmath4 corresponding to the number of virtual - photon exchanges .    before the 1970s",
    ", investigations of qed effects in atomic systems were mainly focused on low-@xmath7 atoms such as hydrogen and helium . in these systems ,",
    "in addition to the expansion parameter @xmath4 , there is another small parameter @xmath3 , which characterizes the strength of the nuclear binding field .",
    "because of this , most early calculations of qed effects were based on the expansion in both @xmath4 and @xmath3 .",
    "such calculations produced accurate results for hydrogen and a few light atoms but provided little or no information about qed effects in high-@xmath7 ions , in which the parameter @xmath3 approaches unity .    in 1974 p.  j.  mohr reported his pioneering calculations of the electron self - energy to all orders in the parameter @xmath3 @xcite .",
    "these calculations , together with their extension to the @xmath1 states several years later @xcite , have greatly increased the theoretical accuracy of the lamb shift in hydrogenlike ions .",
    "the results of these studies were used as a basis of the compilations by mohr @xcite and by johnson and soff @xcite , which for many years remained the standard references on hydrogenlike ions .    during the decades following the compilation by johnson and soff , many calculations of various effects contributing to the lamb shift of hydrogenlike atoms were performed .",
    "most notably , the vacuum - polarization was calculated to all orders in @xmath3 in refs .",
    "@xcite , the nuclear size correction to the self - energy was obtained in ref .",
    "@xcite , the nuclear recoil correction was evaluated to the first order in @xmath14 but to all orders in @xmath3 in ref .",
    "@xcite , the nuclear polarization correction was obtained in ref .",
    "@xcite , the two - loop self - energy was calculated to all orders in @xmath3 in refs .",
    "@xcite . alongside with the above",
    "mentioned nonperturbative calculations , the hydrogen theory was developed further within the @xmath3-expansion approach .",
    "the most notable achievements were the calculation of the @xmath15 two - loop contribution @xcite and the calculations of the two - loop corrections to order @xmath16 @xcite .",
    "theoretical advances of the last decades were complemented by the experimental progress in high - precision spectroscopy of highly charged ions @xcite .",
    "modern experiments access hydrogenlike ions along the whole periodic table up to uranium and study the strong - nuclear - field regime of the bound - state qed . measurements of the ground - state lamb shift in the hydrogenlike uranium have rapidly progressed during last years , achieving the accuracy of @xmath17  ev  @xcite , which corresponds to the fractional error of 1% of the lamb shift . further advance is anticipated in these experiments , which will make them sensitive to the nonperturbative two - loop qed effects .",
    "the goal of the present work is to summarize theoretical developments of the last decades and to compile an up - to - date tabulation of the energy levels of the @xmath0 and @xmath1 states of hydrogenlike atoms with the nuclear charges @xmath2 .",
    "the total energy of a hydrogenlike atom is a sum of the rest mass of the atom and the electron binding energy @xmath18 , @xmath19 where @xmath20 is the nuclear mass , @xmath21 is the electron mass , and @xmath22 is the speed of light .",
    "the dominant part of the electron binding energy of a hydrogenlike atom can be calculated analytically .",
    "several closed - form analytical results are well - known , namely : ( i ) the dirac equation for the point - nucleus coulomb potential can be solved exactly to all orders in @xmath3 , ( ii ) the nonrelativistic two - body problem for the point particles can be solved for arbitrary masses @xmath20 and @xmath21 , ( iii ) the recoil correction within the breit approximation can be obtained analytically to first order in @xmath14 but to all orders in @xmath3 .",
    "it is natural to separate out these analytical contributions to the binding energy , with the rest being called as the lamb shift .",
    "so , we write the electron binding energy of a hydrogenlike atom as @xmath23 where @xmath24 is the dirac point - nucleus biding energy , @xmath25 is the leading nuclear mass ( recoil ) correction , and @xmath26 is the lamb shift .",
    "the dirac point - nucleus binding energy @xmath24 is given by @xmath27\\,,\\end{aligned}\\ ] ] where @xmath28 @xmath29 is the radial quantum number , @xmath30 is the principal quantum number , and @xmath31 is the angular momentum - parity quantum number .    the leading recoil correction @xmath25 is written as @xmath32c^2\\,\\frac{({z\\alpha})^2}{2n^2 }   \\nonumber \\\\ = & \\   mc^2\\,\\frac{m}{m}\\frac{({z\\alpha})^2}{2n^2 } - m_r c^2 \\,\\left ( \\frac{m}{m}\\right)^2 \\ ,     \\frac{({z\\alpha})^2}{2n^2}\\,,\\end{aligned}\\ ] ] where @xmath33 and @xmath34 is the reduced mass of the electron .",
    "@xmath35 consists of two parts .",
    "the first part is the first - order ( in @xmath14 ) recoil correction as derived from the breit equation @xcite , whereas the second part is the nonrelativistic reduced - mass correction of second and higher orders in @xmath14 .",

    "we note that the separation ( [ eq1a ] ) is not unique and different definitions of the lamb shift can be found in the literature . in the high-@xmath7 region ,",
    "the recoil effect is a small correction , so it is often included into the lamb shift @xcite . for low-@xmath7 ions ,",
    "however , the nuclear recoil is a large effect , so its leading part is usually separated out . in the theory of hydrogen",
    "it is common @xcite to define @xmath25 in a slightly different way , which is based on the result derived from the modified dirac equation @xcite .",
    "the difference with the present definition is very small and is noticeable for the case of hydrogen and he@xmath8 only .",
    "we prefer to define @xmath25 in the form of eq .",

    "we also note a small difference of definitions of the lamb shift in the present compilation and in the tabulation by johnson and soff @xcite , which is of no importance at the level of accuracy of ref .",

    "the _ vacuum - polarization _ is the qed shift of the energy levels due to production of a virtual @xmath82 pair .",
    "the dominant part of the one - loop vacuum polarization is known as the uehling correction  @xcite .",
    "the uehling approximation treats the virtual @xmath82 pair as freely propagating , i.e. , undisturbed by the nuclear field .",
    "this treatment takes into account the virtual @xmath82 pair to the leading order in the coupling constant @xmath3 .",
    "the remaining part of the one - loop vacuum - polarization is referred to as the wichmann - kroll correction @xcite .",
    "the wichmann - kroll potential contains all higher - order terms in @xmath3 , @xmath83 with @xmath84 . according to the furry theorem",
    ", there are no contributions @xmath83 with even powers of @xmath30 .    the one - loop uehling vacuum - polarization correction for the point nuclear charge",
    "is represented as @xcite @xmath85 where @xmath86 and @xmath87 is the higher - order remainder .",
    "the calculation of @xmath87 is quite straightforward and can be performed up to arbitrary accuracy .",
    "the results listed in the present compilation are obtained by our own calculations ; they fully agree with other values published previously in the literature , e.g. , in ref .",
    "@xcite .",
    "the _ one - loop wichmann - kroll vacuum - polarization correction _ for the point nuclear charge is parameterized as @xmath88 unlike the uehling contribution , a direct calculation of the wichmann - kroll correction is a non - trivial task .",
    "first calculations of this correction to all orders in @xmath3 were reported by soff and mohr for the shell model of the nuclear charge distribution @xcite and by manakov and co - workers for the point nuclear charge @xcite .",
    "accurate calculations of the wichmann - kroll correction were later performed also by other groups @xcite .",
    "recently , the problem of calculating the wichmann - kroll correction for the point nuclear charge was greatly simplified by the high - precision approximation formulas reported by manakov and nekipelov @xcite .",
    "these formulas are based on the analytical expansions of whittaker functions and approximate the exact point - nucleus wichmann - kroll potential with a relative accuracy of @xmath89 or better for nuclear charges @xmath90 . since this precision is fully sufficient in the context of the present compilation , we used the formulas from ref .",
    "@xcite to calculate the wichmann - kroll correction for the point nuclear charge .",
    "the results obtained in this way are in agreement with the direct calculations of the wichmann - kroll correction for the point nuclear charge @xcite .",

    "a numerical calculation of @xmath176 is quite straightforward for most ions . in the present tabulations we use results of our own calculations .",
    "they were performed by solving the dirac equation with two independent methods , the one based on the dual kinetic balance approach @xcite and the other based on the radial package @xcite .",
    "comparison of the results obtained by these two methods was used as a check of numerical accuracy . for low-@xmath7 ions ,",
    "the fns contribution becomes very small , and the calculations are complicated by large numerical cancellations . in order to overcome this problem , we implemented the dual kinetic balance method in the quadruple ( 32-digit ) arithmetics , which allowed us to perform accurate numerical determination of the fns corrections for all ions including hydrogen .",
    "numerical values obtained in this way were checked against the results obtained by analytical formulas from ref .",

    "experimental values of the root - mean - square ( rms ) nuclear charge radii used in the compilation were taken from ref .",
    "@xcite . in the rare cases when no experimental data were available , we used the standard approximation formula @xcite ( in fermi ) @xmath256 and ascribed the uncertainty of 10% to this value of @xmath168 .",

    ".    it might be instructive to compare the individual contributions to the lamb shift in the present compilation with the corresponding results from the compilation by johnson and soff @xcite as tabulated 30 years ago .",
    "such comparison for three selected ions with @xmath263 , @xmath63 , and @xmath77 is shown in table  [ tab : js ] .",

    "@xcite .",
    "we observe that the main change in the theoretical values for the total lamb shift in medium- and high-@xmath7 region is due to the two - loop qed corrections , which were unknown at the time of the previous compilation .",
    "after the calculations @xcite have been carried out , both the sign and the magnitude of the two - loop qed contribution turned out to be different from what had been estimated .",
    "another important difference comes from the fns correction , which is due to changes in the experimental values of the nuclear charge radii .",
    "apart from that , we observe good agreement with the results from ref .",
    "@xcite for most of the contributions .",
    "the total theoretical accuracy of the lamb shift is considerably improved ( typically , by a factor of 5 ) as compared to the previous compilation .",
    "the results for hydrogen in tables  [ tab : lamb ] and [ tab : energy ] are given mainly for completeness , since the hydrogen theory is critically reviewed and regularly updated in the codata adjustment of fundamental constants @xcite .",
    "the theoretical values of the hydrogen transition energies listed in table  [ tab : energy ] are consistent with the codata 2010 adjustment @xcite and in agreement with the ( much more accurate ) garching experimental result for the @xmath259 transition in hydrogen @xcite .",
    "the comparison with hydrogen experiments can not be used as a test of theoretical calculations , since hydrogen spectroscopy is used for the determination of the rydberg constant and the proton charge radius .    in table",
    "[ tab : comparison ] we compare the theoretical predictions for the lamb shift and transition energies in hydrogenlike ions with the available experimental results .",
    "the lamb shift for the @xmath49 state is much larger than for the excited states but difficult to access in an experiment .",
    "it is usually determined experimentally by studying @xmath264 transitions . since the lamb shift forms only a small part of these transition energies , very precise measurements in the x - ray regime are required .",
    "the highest fractional accuracy so far was achieved in the experiment on u@xmath265 @xcite , which has reached the sensitivity of 1% to the @xmath49 lamb shift .",
    "accurate measurements were reported also for other ions , notably , for ar@xmath266 @xcite and for ni@xmath267 @xcite , with the fractional errors of 1.2% and 2.0% of the lamb shift , correspondingly .",
    "the @xmath11 lamb shift is approximately eight times smaller than the @xmath49 lamb shift , but it is easier to access experimentally since the @xmath11 and the @xmath268 levels are close in energy . the @xmath260 and @xmath269 transitions are accessible to laser spectroscopy over a wide region of @xmath7 using far - infrared to ultraviolet lasers . a serious problem , however , is the natural width of the transitions that grows with @xmath7 as @xmath270 . because of this , accurate experimental results for @xmath271 transitions are available mostly for low- and medium-@xmath7 ions",
    ".    one of the most accurate experiments of this kind is the measurement of the classical @xmath260 lamb shift in he@xmath8 @xcite , which reached the sensitivity to qed effects on the level of @xmath272 parts per million .",
    "unfortunately , this measurement disagrees with theory by about two standard deviations .",
    "accurate measurements of the @xmath11 lamb shift have been also reported for @xmath273n@xmath274 @xcite , @xmath275p@xmath276 @xcite , and @xmath277s@xmath278 @xcite , with a precision of @xmath279-@xmath280 of the lamb shift .",
    "in this paper we tabulated theoretical energies and energy - level separations of @xmath0 and @xmath1 states of the hydrogenlike atoms with the nuclear charges @xmath2 . a detailed breakdown of individual qed corrections to the lamb shift of the @xmath49 , @xmath11 , @xmath12 , and @xmath121 states is provided for each atom .",
    "the main sources of uncertainty of the theoretical energy levels in hydrogenic systems are presently the two - loop qed corrections and the lack of detailed knowledge of the nuclear charge distributions .",
    "both these problems can be addressed in future in theoretical and experimental studies .",
    "principal limitations of the theoretical description are associated with the dynamical nuclear effects , such as the nuclear polarization .",
    "accurate calculations of such effects would require detailed understanding of the nuclear structure , which is presently lacking .",
    "so far , however , the uncertainty due to nuclear polarization is not the dominant source of the theoretical error for most of the hydrogenlike atoms .",
    "it is therefore likely that the precision of the theoretical description of the hydrogenlike systems will be improved further in the future .",
